    "lc1, lc2, lc3 = np.zeros(len(tpf.time)), np.zeros(len(tpf.time)), np.zeros(len(tpf.time))\n",
    "for i in range(len(tpf.time)):\n",
    "    lc1[i] = apr.CircularAperture((1008.5 - tpf.column, 687.5 - tpf.row), r=1).do_photometry(tpf.flux[i])[0]\n",
    "    lc2[i] = apr.CircularAperture((1008.5 - tpf.column, 689.5 - tpf.row), r=1).do_photometry(tpf.flux[i])[0]\n",
    "    lc3[i] = apr.CircularAperture((1012.5 - tpf.column, 688.5 - tpf.row), r=1).do_photometry(tpf.flux[i])[0]"
   ]

   "source": [
    "The messy part below (which will soon be encapsulated as a class called `KeplerPRFPhotometry`) iterates over all frames of the target pixel file, solving an optimization problem for every frame, and storing the results of the optmization in the arrays declared below."
   ]

    "xc1_hat, xc2_hat, xc3_hat = [], [], []\n",
    "yc1_hat, yc2_hat, yc3_hat = [], [], []\n",
    "f1_hat, f2_hat, f3_hat = [], [], []\n",
    "bkg_hat = []\n",
    "residuals = []\n",
    "loglike = []\n",
    "prf1, prf2, prf3 = [], [], []\n",
    "best_fit_params = []\n",
    "kepprf = KeplerPRF(tpf.channel, (tpf.shape[1], tpf.shape[2]),\n",
    "                   tpf.column, tpf.row,\n",
    "                   prf_files_dir=\"/Users/jvmirca/.pyke/kepler-prf-calibration-data/\")\n",
    "for i in tqdm.tqdm(range(len(tpf.time))):\n",
    "    x0 = np.array((lc1[i] - np.pi * bkg[i], # Flux for first source\n",
    "                   lc2[i] - np.pi * bkg[i], # Flux for second source\n",
    "                   lc3[i] - bkg[i],         # Flux for the third source\n",
    "                   1008.5, 1008.5, 1012.5,  # Column centroid for first and second sources\n",
    "                   687.5, 689.5, 688.5,     # Row centroid for first and second sources\n",
    "                   bkg[i]))                 # Background\n",
    "    logL = PoissonLikelihood(tpf.flux[i], kepprf.evaluate)\n",
    "    result = logL.fit(x0, method='Powell', options={'xtol':1e-6, 'ftol':1e-6})\n",
    "    best_fit_params = np.append(best_fit_params, result.x)\n",
    "    loglike = np.append(loglike, logL.evaluate(result.x))\n",
    "    f1_hat = np.append(f1_hat, result.x[0])\n",
    "    f2_hat = np.append(f2_hat, result.x[1])\n",
    "    f3_hat = np.append(f3_hat, result.x[2])\n",
    "    xc1_hat = np.append(xc1_hat, result.x[3])\n",
    "    xc2_hat = np.append(xc2_hat, result.x[4])\n",
    "    xc3_hat = np.append(xc3_hat, result.x[5])\n",
    "    yc1_hat = np.append(yc1_hat, result.x[6])\n",
    "    yc2_hat = np.append(yc2_hat, result.x[7])\n",
    "    yc3_hat = np.append(yc3_hat, result.x[8])\n",
    "    bkg_hat = np.append(bkg_hat, result.x[9])\n",
    "    prf1 = np.append(prf1, kepprf.prf_model[0])\n",
    "    prf2 = np.append(prf2, kepprf.prf_model[1])\n",
    "    prf3 = np.append(prf3, kepprf.prf_model[2])\n",
    "    residuals = np.append(residuals, tpf.flux[i] - kepprf.evaluate(*result.x))"
   ]
